It turns your Windows device with a camera into a handy scanner, suitable for scanning various documents like contracts, articles, business cards, notes, receipts, warranty papers etc. Image capture is done with the help of Real-Time Edge Detection (auto crop).\r\n\r\nThis scanner app also excels in import options. It imports variety of document formats, such as odt, ods, odp, csv, svg, hwp and many others. Both scanned and imported documents can be visually enhanced using different filters offered by ScanWritr. \r\n\r\nEdit scans and imports as an image, add signature, annotation, use eraser or pen and fill out the blanks using writing tool. Scan and convert the document to PDF or JPG, save it to your phone’s gallery, send it via e-mail, fax, Facebook, Twitter or other social media. You can also print it (with the help of Cloud Print) or save it to Google Drive, One Drive, Drop Box, Box or your other preferred cloud storage service (requires a working cloud client) - all in the comfort of your own mobile device!\r\n\r\nScanWritr's feature list:\r\n●\tCamera-based Document Scanner (scan documents with your phone)\r\n●\tReal-Time Edge Detection (Auto Crop)\r\n●\tImage Enhancement\r\n●\tDocument Import (MS Office, Open Office, Libre Office, Hancom/Hangul etc.)\r\n●\tAdding Text to Pictures & Form Filling (Writing Tool)\r\n●\tSigning (signature tool)\r\n●\tText Annotation (Marker Tool)\r\n●\tFax (outbound, requires the purchase of fax tokens)\r\n●\tPrint (via Google Cloud Print)\r\n●\tCloud Sharing (via DropBox, Google Drive, One Drive, Box etc. - a working cloud client with support for JPEG/PDF required)\r\n●\tPDF Converter (convertst documents to PDF, converts pdf to JPG) \r\n●\tSocial Media Connectivity (share via Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn etc.)\r\n\r\nScan & Import\r\nScanWritr allows you to use the camera on your mobile device as a document scanner.
